# Graph Report - LUMIERA  (2026-07-22)

## Corpus Check
- 2696 files · ~12,788,341 words
- Verdict: corpus is large enough that graph structure adds value.

## Summary
- 18652 nodes · 32236 edges · 1356 communities (1239 shown, 117 thin omitted)
- Extraction: 99% EXTRACTED · 1% INFERRED · 0% AMBIGUOUS · INFERRED: 312 edges (avg confidence: 0.69)
- Token cost: 0 input · 0 output

## Graph Freshness
- Built from commit: `15c552ca`
- Run `git rev-parse HEAD` and compare to check if the graph is stale.
- Run `graphify update .` after code changes (no API cost).
